# Alpha Things - 参考原著

> 用途：风格参考，提炼英文狼人文写作规范

Prologue	
Screams echoed in the empty mansion, a storm raging, winds howling, and the shy thundering with anger and rage. this was not right, not in the slightest, not when the future of the entire species depends on it.
The Gods were angry, that was a given.
This is not the time that the queen wanted her child to be born, she wanted him to enter this world with the sun shining down on him with its soft rays and birds chirping happily, and the whole mansion would celebrate the birth of their king with love, but there are some things that not even The Kings and Queens can control.
The wailing Queen cried out in pain, praying this torture would end and she can finally hold her baby in her arms. The King was by her side, helping her by just staying by her side. he held her hand kissing her forehead whispering encouragement in her ears hoping to ease her pain by holding her arms praying that he could somehow, transfer all that pain to himself.
Doctors and Nurses littered the place, running around doing things they were supposed to, they did everything in their power to help deliver the baby, as much as they hate to do this, they had to do it. they look at each other having a silent conversation amount themselves as to why the baby wasn't here yet, or what it shouldn't be here, they didn't let out a peep fearing the wrath of their king.
""Lucian, please promise me something,"" the queen begged, holding her husband's hand, she had a sheen layer of perspiration on her beautiful face, the king who was a husband right about now, leaned forward to kiss his wife's hand 
""Anything, my love,"" he assured her looking at her with deep love and affection
she swallows a scream as the labor pain hit her ten times harder, the kid was on a warpath, and its first victim was his mother "" Promise me you will love our son, just the way you love me, and"" ahhh she screamed painfully before she could complete her sentence "" promise me you won't believe the superstition that is going around about our son, promise me,"" she begged him to accept her wishes, hoping he would value it above everything.
""I promise you, my love, we will together raise this child with love and care and won't let anything ever happen to him, as long as we both shall live,"" he kissed her head with admiration at this moment of life and death her only worry was her unborn child.
The queen gave out another heart-wrenching scream that enhanced the volume of the thundering bombardment. as time passed the shield of silence was shattered with a cry of a baby, an innocent-looking infant crying its heart out, the doctors and nurses held the beautiful wailing baby in their arms as they cut the umbilical cord, and clean the bloody baby.
""It's a boy, my Highness"" the doctor announced with a fake smile but the new parents didn't care about that, not a lot of people liked children, who will rule over them someday.
The King looked at his spent wife, tired, and yet she had this warm smile on her face that boosted his pride, he leaned down to kiss his wife on her lips only this time they didn't respond, his heart broke at the sight of his still wife.
He let out a cry, his inner wolf howled in pain at the loss of his soulmate, he whimpered and wailed at his loss, he held the corpse of his mate and cried like a baby, only then did he realize that he had a son as well.
He called out to the doctor who was too quiet for his liking, ""Where is my son?"" he growled at the empty cradle, he might be in pain but he knew he was yet to be handed his child, which the doctor failed to do so.
""My King, the baby is weak his lungs are failing, some of our best doctors are working hard to help him"" the doctor stuttered but she seemed to be more nervous than scared.
""Help him, do whatever you can, and save my son,"" he ordered the shivering doctor, she nodded her head and left the room only for it to fill with an air of sadness.
He held his dead wife in his arms and pulled her closer kissing her head "" I promise you, my love, he will be loved and respected, and one day he will rule this world as one of the greatest kings, anyone has ever seen,"" he let his wife go after placing one last kiss, this was a goodbye.
He walked into the ICU for infants only to see his boy be attached to life support, the sight pained him to the next level, the loss of his wife hadn't fully hit him yet, and he wasn't ready to lose his son as well.
""My King?"" the five feet something doctor called out to the six feet something pureblood werewolf. she was scared to announce the next news she had discovered 
""What is it?"" he asked not losing sight of his son, he might be small and premature but he was a sight to be held, a true beauty just like his mother.
""We found something about the prince, my King, I don't think you will like it,"" she said not looking at his face but rather the white tiles.
The King had been preparing for this day, he knew the risks of having the baby, so that was the reason he had converted the entire floor of his mansion into a hospital so that his wife and child wouldn't have to go away for treatment
 
""Just tell me, I don't desire you to sugar coat it as well, say what you have to say,"" he stood there looking at his son not spearing the doctor as a single glance 
""My King, I'm afraid you will not like this news,"" she paused but the pause didn't receive any response ""he is born without a wolf my lord, he is born with a beast,"""
2	The Beast	"Age three

the boy grew up to be truly beautiful and innocent, the boy would make anyone fall to their knees with just a smile, and the boy had his father's eyes. blue and grey, one look at them, and anyone will be under a spell but people always talk, no one liked to come across a beast, a devil, an abomination. 

lots of people or the maids in the mansion stayed clear of the boy, nobody addressed the boy as the crowned prince, he was hated and spat at but the boy smiled at everything that spared him a look.

the King tried to stay with the boy as much as he could but that was not enough, the king had assigned wet nurses, and a nanny to watch over the boy but he would wail and cry alone in the middle of the day or night, sometimes he would be left alone to fend for himself, but what a three-year-old innocent child could do.

one day the boy left his designated room to look for his father, looking for someone familiar and someone who loved him no matter what. he walked the vast halls, trying not to wonder, but yet he did.

he walked into a room where there were lots of paintings and huge chairs, but no one in sight. the boy heard voices beyond the room from a single door, at the age of three, the child was way more mature than any other seven years old, boy. he walked to the door and peeked in.

there he saw three ministers talking to his nanny, he opened his mouth to call out to her, but he remembered that the last he did it she ignored him and went away, so he just stood there watching them.

""Take this and make sure he consumes it before midnight, the boy will not live to see the next sunrise. the King is stupid to let the beast, live but we cannot sit and watch that thing grow up and destroy our kingdom, hurry don't let anyone see you,"" the grand minister ushered the maid away, and she was coming right at him.

the boy ran away with his little legs to hide beneath the large table, he thought over what he had witnessed but didn't know what had happened.

he waited for everyone to leave before he crawled out of his hiding spot, he wonders around again but couldn't find his father anywhere in the mansion, he then used his werewolf senses to try to find his father's scent, and he caught on to the scent and followed it. the scent led him to a huge room at the end of the hall. 

he walked in the door and found a beautiful room with a huge bed and windows, his sense went haywire when a comforting aura surrounded him, his instincts forced him to climb up and engulf himself with the scent. he pulled out the duvet cover off the bed and pulled it all around him. it gave him so much comfort like he knew who it belongs to and yet he didn't at the same time. he felt himself relax and after a long time in his three years of life, he slept, with a smile on his face.

he woke up to chaos around him, he rubbed his sleepy eyes, and he yawned loving the warmth of the duvet blanket. he was about to nod off again but the growling and yelling distract him. he crawls out of the room but held the blanket closer to his body. the voices grew louder with every step he took.

""where is my son?"" the King roared angrily scaring the servants in front of him

""Papa?"" he yawned rubbing his eyes and looking at his father who was growling with anger, he had half shifted into his wolf his eyes blood red, his claws out, with hair growing on his skin. his father's face snapped in his direction and his body language changed aggressively, he shifted back to his human form, he shed his hair and his claws retreated before he ran to hold his child in his arms.

""where were you, my child? I was scared something bad happened"" he kissed his chubby cheeks, and the child giggled as his father's beard scratched his face. then he stopped as his child's scent was mixed with his mate's scent, a scent he knew too well. he looked at his son trying to find the source. he saw the blanket his child was clenching in his small hands

""Where did you find this, my child?"" the child clenched the blanket tighter again afraid his father would take it away.

""it's mine, Papa I found it"" his father smiled down at his child's innocence he kissed his head and hugged the child tighter, he was happy his child craved his mate's scent.

""let's go, I'll take you to see your mother, "" he kissed his soft head again. the boy yawned again and laid his head on his father's shoulder snuggling into his warmth.

the King walked back to the room his child had fallen asleep in, King closed the door and carried his child towards a huge portrait, and stood in front of it

""This is your mother, child, you look just like her,"" the boy looked awed at the beautiful woman in front of him.

""She so pretty, Papa "" the child exclaimed giggling cheerfully.

""yes my child, she is very pretty just like you,"" he blooped his small nose 

""Papa? am I a bad child?"" he asked chewing at the end of the blanket.

The King raised an eyebrow at his son's question "" why do you say that? did someone say that to you?"" he inquired 

""My nanny and three other men said some bad things about me, he also gave the nanny something in a small bottle,"" the boy spoke of the matter playing with the blanket not realizing how severe the accusation was.

The King stiffened as the words left his son's mouth, he kissed the head of his beautiful son, "" You are not bad my child, it's the people who don't understand how to differentiate between good and evil, you, my son, are the nicest boy I have ever met, don't let anyone tell you otherwise, ""

that night the child slept in his mother's room snuggling into her scent not knowing how his father had brutally executed the four people, someone who would go to such lengths as to murder an innocent child.

the screams and cries of the four people echoed in the basement of the mansion, unknown to the people living above. the King kept his promise, and he intended to do so for the rest of his life, protecting his precious child."
3	The Alpha	"Age 6

Alejandro woke up in the middle of the night feeling suffocated, it was getting hard for him to breathe, he tried to push the pillow out of his face but it didn't budge, he was losing his grip on the pillow, his legs kicking away the person trying to suffocate him, he closed his eyes, his head aching with lack of oxygen his legs stiffened and he passed out before he could do anything

A scream woke the entire mansion from its deep sleep, people were running to the source of the scream, everyone stood shocked at the scene in front of them, the King woke from his slumber to the chaos that took place in his mansion. he put on his robe and strode towards the noise. the noises led him towards his son's room. fear woke within him thinking something bad had happened to his precious son, he walked faster towards the door and found all the servants standing at the door, they parted ways to make room for the King to address what had happened, he froze in his place watching the scene in front of him. 

His son was sitting on the floor of his room, covered in blood and the torn corpse of the maid lay next to his son, which frightened him more watching the look on his son's face, his eyes had turned completely black, fangs and claws were out in the open for everyone to see. and the look on his face, he had no remorse, no guilt, and no sadness.

""My child,"" the king exclaimed the boy looked at his father and the fangs and claws retreated but his eyes stayed the same.

""She tried to hurt us, Papa,"" the voice was different than his, deeper which led him to believe that it was his inner beast talking. 

The whispers and murmurs surrounded the area "" He is a monster""

""Murderer, ""

""Beast ""

""Killer""

""Demon""

""Devil,""

""Evil,""

""Abomination ""

The whispers grew as the king walked to his son, picking him up and carrying him in his arms, the boy wrapped himself in his father's embrace and buried himself in his warmth.

""One more word about this and none of you will see the next light, someone cleans the area, I don't want the blood to stain the floor,"" he carried his son out of the room to his bedroom, he baths his son trying to rid the blood off his skin, he threw the bloody clothes into the hamper. the fresh-showered Alejandro glazed at his father waiting for his reaction.

""I'm not a monster, Papa, I took over because she tried to hurt us, I didn't mean to kill her, I'm sorry, Papa "" the child cried looking at his feet that dangled on the bed.

his father patted his head dry, ""I know, my child and I'm proud of you for defending yourself, you are not a monster, baby, you are a very powerful boy, sometimes people are scared of more powerful people than them, but you have to promise me that next time you will protect yourself but only when it's the more severe situation, and killing comes last, never hurt anyone weaker than you, never bully anyone, react only when things have evaluated into a threat."" he explained trying not to sound too strict 

the boy nodded his head trying to understand every word his father said to him.

the next day was worst, the entire pre-school knew about the events that had taken place last night, the king had asked Alejandro to take a day off but he had made a friend and didn't want to miss a day, he finally had made a friend. 

he walked to the class but everyone looking at him accusingly, he felt small, he walked to his desk and sat next to his friend and smiled but his friend didn't reciprocate, his smile turned into a frown and he looked ahead trying not to think too much about it. the teachers didn't spare him a look even when he had raised his hand, he kept quiet not knowing what to do.

During PE things had escalated to the next level, the boys around him bullied him for being a monster, they called him a murderer but one boy had done the worst.

there was this one boy who was everyone's favorite, everyone loved him and he took its complete advantage.

""This is not his first murder, he killed his mother when he was born, he is not a prince but a monster, he should not be our king, I promise you, Alejandro, I will take your throne and throw you in dungeons to rot,"" the little green-eyed boy shrieked angrily, he was the son of the second most powerful werewolf in the world, his father has been trying to take over the throne but had failed on many instances.

Alejandro had tears in his eyes, it was hard for him to talk about his mother's death it was a sore spot.

for the first time in his life he felt rage, the anger he felt was beyond his control, he didn't know what he felt but he didn't like the way the boy spoke about his mother.

""shut up"" he spoke slowly not raising his voice, the young boy didn't receive the threat 

he mocked the prince ""what? I didn't hear that?"" he laughed with his friends

""I said shut up!"" he growled ragefully, the roar echoed the playground everyone felt chills down their spine with the amount of power it contained.

""No!"" the young boy replied with the same intensity ""you don't order me around, you are a killer, a monster, my Papa told me not to tolerate your stuck-up behavior,"" he yelled not caring about how Alejandro's eyes changed color.

the kids around them gasped looking at their prince with his beast taking control of his body. the young boy took a step back looking at his eyes but stood his ground.

""stop talking,"" he growled fisting his hands so the claws don't come out

""no!"" the young boy yelled before charging toward him and punching his face with everything he got.

the prince stumbled across but held his ground, his face had turned to the ground, his jaw hurting this was when he lost control over his beast.

the beast roared furiously taking control over his body and charged toward the young boy, he tried to punch him but couldn't bring it in himself, so he pushed him not realizing thy his claws were out and he did more damage than he intends to, he had clawed his little chest, the big howled in pain and the teachers rushed towards the bleeding boy. 

Alejandro took back control over his body but it was too late, the damage was already done, he tried to apologize by waking up him but the teachers and other kids circled the wounded boy, and the accusations they had in their eyes were true, it hurt his little heart to receive such strong emotions.

he looked at the young boy and saw the same expression but it had more hatred in his, the pang he felt in his heart had double the effect.

He was a real monster
"
4	His Regret	"Alejandro felt guilty. he never meant to hurt his classmate he was just too angry, he kept his head down the entire way home as the driver drove him back home, he dreaded facing his father because the school had already informed him about the incident that took place today. 

The King was waiting for his son to approach him sitting on the couch staring at Alejandro patiently. Alejandro walked towards his father slowly, he climbed the couch and sat on his father's lap, not facing him.

""look at me, my child"" he pulled his son closer to see his tearful face, he wiped his face clean and waited for his version of the accident

""Papa, I didn't mean for it to happen, he spoke about mama,"" Alejandro hiccups rubbing his leaking eyes, his father sighed trying to understand his misery.

""but that's not how you solve things, Alejandro, violence is never an answer."" Alejandro looked down shamefully. ""the principal is not happy with what happened today, "" 

""Will they punish me, Papa?"" he asked innocently

his father didn't have the heart to tell him that he was rusticated, so he said this instead ""No, my child nobody will ever hurt you, you will study somewhere else, for the time being, you are a special kid Alejandro, you need to control your powers and there is only one place that can happen,"" he said running his fingers in his soft hair

""it is somewhere scary, Papa?"" he asked innocently twiddling with his fingers.

""Not scary, it's a sanctuary, you will train there and live with him for a few years, and when you are. I will bring you back,"" he assured his son, smiling encouragingly.

Alejandro nodded his little head, trying to understand the seriousness of the situation, maybe it's for the best. maybe if he can control his anger he can finally make some friends and people who hate him so much.

""it's done then, you will leave tomorrow to go live with your great grandfather, he lives in the mountains, he is the one who taught two generations of Alpha, you will be fine,"" he patted his son's back and put him down going back to work.

Alejandro walked back to his room looking at the bed of the small car, the wallpaper filled with space, stars, and buzz lighter. everything was too perfect to be true, he then walked to his mother, room and laid on her bed holding her blanket, her fragrance, and her warmth was still present after so many years. 

he snuggles deeper into the blanket and spoke to his mother in a small voice hoping she could hear her ""mommy, I know you can hear me, I want to let you know that I'm not a bad kid, I didn't mean to hurt him or the maid, I didn't even know when or how I hurt her. all I remember is waking up to see blood all over me and her body going cold but I know it's not an excuse. I shouldn't have hurt that boy too but he was being mean mommy, he told me I'm the reason you are not here anymore, and I don't know how to take that. is it true? did I hurt you, mommy? the same way I hurt the maid? I don't know how to understand this. Paps is sending me away to live with my great grandfather, he said he can help me control my powers, and maybe then I can be a better person. maybe just maybe, everyone will love me too, "" he mumbled into the blanket, cocooning himself with its warmth.

He didn't sense his father watching the whole thing with tears filling his eyes, he prayed to the moon goddess to give him the strength to do the right thing, he knew what he was about to do was just too much for his little boy but he had no choice if the incidents kept piling up his would-be deemed to be a true monster, something he didn't want to happen to his only child.

He knew he had to do this even if it broke his heart and shattered his soul, this needs to be done. his grandfather was not the nicest person in the world but he is the only person old enough to know what and why his son possesses this kind of power and rage.

He let his son sleep in his mother's nest and walked away preparing for what was to come tomorrow.

Alejandro woke up late at night, the moon was at its highest peak, he rubbed his sleepy eyes, and realized he had once again slept in his mother's room. he went back to his room trying not to remember last night's accident which reminds him of the boy he hurt today, guilt seeping out of his pores, he decided to apologize to him before he left for who knows how long.

He decided to write an apology letter "" I'm sorry for hurting you, it was not my intention, I hope you forgive me. I'm leaving today and I don't know when I will be back so keep this as a token of my apology "" and signed it with his name and then he put the marble stone he found one-day wondering around the river near his mansion, this stone was one of a kind and it took him a lot of time to find it. 

He thought if he gave him his most prized possession maybe he forgives him and be his friend after coming back.

He knew a lot of tricks of how to sneak out of the mansion without being caught. he was very fast for a kid his age so he ran without alerting the patrols and crossed the border of the silver moon pack, he used his senses to track the boy's house and found it at the edge of the border, he climbed the window of the first room on the left that had his scent the strongest. he saw the boy sleeping peacefully, his chest was wrapped with bandages which sparked the feeling of guilt in Alejandro's heart, slowly and carefully he places the small box with his letter on it next to the boy on his bedside table and with the last look at the boy, he ran back to his house and waited for the next phase of his life to begin 

and it did, for something he did not expect, something he was not ready for.

5	Without Him	"Lorenzo Knight P.O.V

I woke up groggy with a headache making its presence known, the pounding in my head was too much for me to bear, slowly I open my right eye and shut it quickly when the sharp rays of sunlight hit my eyes, I groan miserably when a giggle made its way to my ear, I open my eyes to see the blonde gazing at me with adoration, ah then it hit me. the memories of last night, Rose threw an end-of-summer party and I got drunk enough to hook up with her, yes, I slept with Rose.

""Good morning, "" she whispered leaning to kiss my lips, I move away and get up not caring that I was completely naked. I keep looking for my clothes and finally found them under the bed, she watched me with annoyed eyes, ""at least, try to pretend like you felt something last night, doesn't make me feel like a whore,"" she exclaims wrapping the sheets around her body while sitting up straight.

I smirked at her leaning towards her, she leaned too expecting a kiss but I pulled my belt from underneath her leg, and I pulled it away getting a squeak out of her as she fell, I had zero regards towards her or any of the girls I had slept with.

""Don't take it personally, it's just sex"" I winked at her and left the room, dodging the pillow she threw at me.

""You are a fucking dick, Lorenzo!"" she screamed got me chucking in amusement, I walked down the stairs and see my best friend Joshua spread out on the recliner passed out with a beer bottle in his hand.

I kick his leg making him fall to the floor with a thud, he glared at me holding his side growling furiously ""I was sleeping, you asshole"" he cursed then groaned holding his head, the hangover was a nasty thing.

""let's go, I'll buy you a Starbucks on the way, we have school today, remember, "" I said picking up his jacket and throwing it on his face.

he glared at me one last time "" I'm gonna get the most expensive coffee there is, just so you know"" he Sassed walking towards the door, a lot of people had already left due to today being our first day of high school.

I sighed knowing he would do that and more, he is such a drama Queen,  I follow him to my car and we drive to the nearest Starbucks and get all the greasy food to cure our hangover.

We had privileges as the Alpha and beta of the strongest pack in the world, well second but not for long, our bags and stuff were already there in our locker at school, all we had to do was make our presence known and all is done.

I park my Audi R8 in my parking spot and get out in style, we had fresh clothes in our locker too by the desperate girls in the schools and the pack, I don't say anything because who doesn't like being pampered.

We grab the fresh clothes and shower in the school's locker room, after a much-needed shower we made our way to our second glass because we had already missed the first class.

Everywhere we go we see people murmuring around us, we thought it was the usual thing but by the time the lunch rolled in something was wrong, this was not the usual fan girls kind of murmurs this was different. a couple more of my friends join us during lunch and they had the same look.

""ok, spill it out. is it about the party last night? I don't remember doing anything freaky to get this much attention,"" I said, I was annoyed beyond my usual capacity.

""So, you are telling me that you don't know?"" Caleb said with surprise written all over his face

 Joshua, smacked him in the head ""that's why we are asking genius "" he chucked but no one joined him.

""Just spill it out already,"" I growled not liking the unwanted suspense.

""He is back, Lorenzo, for good this time,"" Peter said sitting straighter in his seat, there was pin-drop silence at our table none spoke a word.

""ok, guys what's will all the suspense, who is back and why does it matter to us?"" Blake laughed not sensing the tension in the room, he and a couple of other boys were new to the pack, not a lot of people knew the history of this city. 

""You are new to this pack, you don't know anything. it's better if you don't speak, might say something to offend Enzo,"" Peter warned him, his eyes edging him took to take this matter seriously.

""ok, but at least tell me who this person is? and why is he such a big issue? I mean he can't be someone as important as the Alpha of our pack"" he laughs ignoring Peter.

""His name is Alejandro King, he is heir to the throne and Lorenzo's arch enemy, "" Caleb told him 

""Heir to the throne? like he is the next King? our king? man no wonder Enzo hates him, I mean he is the most powerful person there is,"" he said without thinking, and in a flash, my hand was around his throat choking the life out of him.

I growled at him, my wolf taking control to finish him off for assuming the less of us, I bared my fangs at him demanding submission "" he is not your king, I am, submit wolf before I rip open your throat and set an example for all the people who think he is better than me,"" my voice got deeper my wolf was pissed 

Blake leaned his head in submission and my wolf growled one last time before pushing him off, I marched out of the cafeteria not heeding the calls of my friends.

I was pissed, I couldn't think straight, he can't come back now, he was supposed to stay there for the rest of his life. I have never been this angry at anyone before he is the only one that brings out the worst in me.

just thinking about him makes the scar on my chest tingle with pain, he did this to me. I have never been able to get over it, every time I look at my bare chest I find myself weak, he put a scar on me when I was a weak little kid. 

and I promised myself that one day I would return the favor only this time he won't live to see the next day.

He is a monster and monsters, are not Kings, saviors are Kings and I'm a savior and I will be the king."
6	His Return	"Alejandro's POV

We drive into the kingdom border and the familiarity hit me with calmness. I let out a sigh leaning on my seat closing my eyes to relax.

""You must have missed home, hmm?"" questioned Sorin, he is the only friend I had managed to make over the last few years, he is a beta wolf, he was abandoned as a child, my great grandfather found him frosting away in the middle of the December, my grandfather might not be the nicest person but he took pity on the frozen child, he can be a lot of things but racism was one thing he was not fond of, so raised him with me and the both of us made the greatest bond.

""Only the air around us, nothing to miss or to be missed around here,"" I said looking out the window, the people were gathering around the car, looking at the car with suspicion and wondering who it might be or if they don't already know, hating or glaring at the car trying to set it on fire.

too much negativity, I know

""Anyone special? I need to watch out for?"" he raised his eyes brows seductively, I hit his arm pushing him away snorting at his antics.

""Not special but you need to watch out for a lot of people, ok? just be on guard, I'm not the most likable person around here"" I explain not making eye contact with him. we have had this conversation before but not too deeply.

""What did you do anyway? "" he asked sitting up straight when the car stopped, and we got out, maids and servants hurried to carry our things and welcome us.

""Murder,"" I said walking away not looking back. I realize he was not walking beside me and turned to face him, I snickered at his stunned expression, as I said, we haven't had this conversation before.

I grabbed his shoulder and pulled him towards my father's office where he was expecting me.

I don't know why he called me back now, but it had to be something important because he was very specific about my early arrival.

I knocked on the door before entering ""hello Father,"" I greeted the stunned man.

King Stefan, was an old man now, with wrinkles decorating his tan face, his blue eyes looked sullen and dull. but when he saw me the surprise was cleared daylight.

""Alejandro? my child"" he walked towards me spreading his arms to envelope me in his warm embrace but I took a step back, avoiding contact, it was impulsive. it was all my training that made me more cautious than ever.

His smile disappeared but he held his ground, he might be a father but he was also a king, he smiled again ""I'm glad you are here, "" I tried smiling not used to the action.

""You sounded urgent, "" I said looking around his office not much had changed. ""what did you need?"" I asked sitting on the couch 

My father looked offended by my question, he should not be I mean he hardly called me in the last ten years and suddenly he wants to play house, not gonna happen.

Sorin coughs awkwardly, my father's head snaps in his direction and he finally addresses the other person in the room.

""Oh, and who might you be young man?"" he asked I sit straight watching him there are not many black people in this kingdom, and if he said anything bad about Sorin, I won't tolerate it.

""The name is Sorin, my King. I was with Alejandro during his stay in the mountains, we trained together,"" Sorin smiled bowing down as he had practiced, I scoffed the both of us are not used to many happy expressions around other people, the thing that he tried to seem nice was beyond me.

""Oh, I'm delighted to meet you boy, finally someone who is willing to be by his side "" he jokes but it annoyed me, Sorin laughed but he was watching me. ""don't make that face Alejandro, you know I'm just kidding,"" he smiles at me.

I look at him seriously ""we aren't that close, to be joking, father. at least not anymore, "" 

""Sorin son, can you give us a moment?"" my father asked him, and he left after bowing down.

He twirled his hair in his fingers "" of course not, that poor thing is dying on its own, I don't like extra work,"" he said with such ease. ""Let's go somewhere else, I have something to show you,"" he got all hyped up and with a snap of his fingers we were in his little hideout 

But what surprised me was all of my people hiding, and waiting for my command were on the floor dead, all of their bodies littered the floor with their blood.

""What the hell have you done?"" I asked him watching everything in horror.

""hmm? oh, this, found them in the woods, and I got bored waiting for you, the floor looks so much better with the color red,"" he commented excitedly.

He was a psycho killer.

""This is going to be so much fun,"" he walked inside the prison and there was a figure sitting on the chair with a blanket on top of him. "" ta, da,"" he said before ripping the blanket off of the person.

Josh, it was Josh.

he was badly beaten and bruised, he could hardly move, he was tired down on the chair.

Alejandro stood up from the ground and marched towards Craig, I tagged along with him, and both of us ganged upon him.

but he was too Fast, he kept having his hands, using spells to avoid our attacks. he grabbed me by my throat and slammed me on the ground, I could feel my spine breaking with the amount of force he was using.

Alejandro turned into his beast and clawed at his back, Craig hissed in pain and let go of me. I shifted into my wolf as well but couldn't reach him because a different wolf attacked me.

It was the fake Omega Rose, she growled at me grinning smugly, I charged at her and bit into her shoulder while digging my claws into her abdomen. she howled in pain, I let her go when I knew she couldn't get up again, my priority was my mate and my best friend's safety.

Alejandro was fighting Craig with all his might and with a huge growl he slashed his claws into his chest ripping into his skin. he was about to end it all but he got tackled by a huge dark wolf.

Alejandro was startled by the sudden intruder and growled when he was it was none other than his childhood best friend, and the mate of the murderous Mage.

""Sorin, stop, please listen to me,"" I shifted back to my human form and grabbed his head, and threw him off Alejandro 

he growled at me furiously and started moving slowly forward, he shifted back to his human form and glared at Alejandro and me. ""What the hell were you about to do? were you going to kill my mate?"" he asks the question directed to Alejandro with betrayal clear in his voice

Craig sat on the ground holding his wounded chest coughing heavily, pretending to be a victim in all this.

Alejandro shifted back and glared at him ""don't you see this? look at all times bodies it's your mate's doing, if he is not stopped now, it's going to be too late later. you and I both know it's true whether you chose to believe in it or not,"" he told Sorin with a firm voice warning him to back down.

""We can deal with it like we always do, we can put him back in the dungeon and punish him accordingly but don't kill him, he is my soul mate after all,"" Sorin pleaded for the sake of his stupid mate.

""Enough, drama,"" Craig stood up and rolled his eyes before moving his hand and trapping us in our places. ""I'm not going back to that filthy place,"" 

Sorin looked at him ""Craig, you need to understand this isn't something to bargain with, Alejandro wasn't joking, he will kill you if you don't surrender,"" he tried to convince his mate but Craig scoffed in disbelief 

""For a beta, you are quite a coward,"" he shook his head disappointed. ""It would have worked if I was your mate, let me tell you a little secret, "" he walked closer to Sorin and whispered in his ear but everyone in the room could hear it.

""We're not mates Sorin, we never were, how do I put it, hmm. I kind of borrowed you for time being,"" he said grinning wickedly.

There was a sudden coldness in the room where it was getting hard to understand what the actual fuck of going on.

He walked away inside the little prison and held Josh's face roughly, he made sure Josh's swollen eyes were directly where he wanted them to be. ""This poor little didn't even know His mate was right there fucking someone else under the same roof as his, "" My eyes widened with the sudden revelation of the things.

Josh was mated to Sorin? how?

""Must be heartbreaking, not knowing your mate was right there while you mourned for a mate yourself. pity, pity,"" he tisked amusingly.

I turned my head to look at Sorin and he was frozen, his face paled as the secrets kept unraveling. I glanced at my mate and found him looking at me.

""What do we do now?"" I asked him through our link.

""Do you trust me?"" he asked back his eyes moving between Craig, Josh, and Sorin.

""Always,"" was my instant reply.

""Then let's do it,"" he said before breaking out of Craig's hold with ease. his transformation has granted him various powers that including immunity to dark magic.

He growled before using his hidden weapon and grabbing Craig by his hair and slamming him on the wall before biting his neck and chewing off the meat off his shoulder.

Cassandra appeared next to me and looked at the fighting duo "" Are you sure? but who do we sacrifice?"" she asked unsurely 

I nodded my head ""I got an idea,"" I said and both of us got to work.

As Alejandro and Craig, were busy fighting I used that opportunity to drop droplets of Alejandro's blood on the floor with Cassandra's help, she used her magic to spread the blood on the floor in a circle around them 

""We still need a source though,"" she kept saying that and stopped when I showed her the solution ""that works too,"" she said closing her eyes and mumbling the spells.

the winds howled in the middle of the woods where the cabin was located, and the atmosphere, in the room changed as everything around the room was smashed to the ground.

62	his end 2	"Alejandro growled at Craig as he kept struggling in his hands ""You can't kill me, I'm immoral,"" he said and choked when Alejandro tighten his hold on his neck.

Cassandra's voice got louder and with one last spell, the fire extended in the circle and engulfed both Craig and Rose in it. he screamed and begged but the fire consumed him, the fire disappeared without a trace and left ashes in its place 

I sighed before hugging Alejandro with all my might ""It's over, it's all over now,"" I said and he hugged me tighter.

The sudden moment in the room snapped us out, we pulled apart to find Sorin sitting on the floor on his knees looking at the ash, and then turning his head to look at badly beaten Josh.

Alejandro went to his friend and held his shoulder ""it is not your fault, he tricked you, Sorin,"" He tried to console him, I went to my best friend and freed him off the ropes and held him straighter. 

he was in and out of consciousness ""I thought my mate was dead, I felt the pain,"" He kept mumbling as I carried him away from the cabin leaving Alejandro and Sorin to speak it out.

I laid him on the hospital bed and held his hand as the tears left his eyes, he burst into tears as the reality hit him, ""I thought he was dead, Lorenzo, I felt the pain my wolf felt the bond breaking,"" he said crying."" how? and why?""

I pulled him in a hug and rubbed his back ""I got you, Josh, we will figure this out,"" I hugged him tighter as he kept weeping.

""What he felt was rejection as his mate marked another, When did you feel the mate bond breaking?"" Cassandra's voice echoed in my head, she must have figured saying it out loud would only hurt him.

"" Last year, June 18th, "" he mumbled looking at the ceiling of the hospital room.

Cassandra closed her eyes and mumbled a few spells, holding Josh's hand, she let it go after opening her eyes, and she let out a small sad smile. Our thoughts went back to the time when Alejandro announced to us that Sorin was found by his grandfather when he was abandoned as a child. they didn't know when he was born so they considered his first birthday as the day he was found, he must have been bigger than a normal baby to be considered older than he looked.

he fell asleep in my arms and I let him sleep on the bed where doctors had cleaned him up and bandaged his wounds

I felt bad for not knowing what my best friend was going through, I was such a bad friend, how could I have missed this.

63	Epilogue	"Five years later

""I'm gonna punch you in the face if you annoy me one more time,"" Alene warned me as both Alejandro and I were holding her hand as she walked down the stairs, fussing over everything she did.

Remember the feisty Omega I met in Florida during my time in the university, well after all the drama with Craig was done. I went back to college and finished up my degree, Alejandro joined me as well and we graduate from college, I graduated first because I was a year ahead of him.

Leon was sad when I told him the truth about Alejandro and my relationship, not the mate thing but that we were in a relationship, and when I got her we were sort of on a break and now we wanted to give it another chance he was heartbroken but he understood where we come from, that didn't last long because he met someone in our final year, the guy was a hybrid, a werewolf, and a vampire, and vampire usually has human mate's so Leon turned out to be his mate.

Everything turned out well after a few years, Josh and Sorin figure out their relationship, they weren't all there but they have been trying to fix their complicated relationship. a couple of months ago they marked each other, and finally, after four horrible years of separation, they were ready to take a step into the real thing, they decided they are the one who will write their story not anyone else.

Sadly Alejandro's father passed away as soon as we were out of college, he fought hard to survive, but cancer was the worst thing that can happen to a strong man. we mourned him every chance we got and prayed for his soul to find peace.

Alejandro officially took the throne with me by his side, we were declared the Kings of the throne since we were both men.

""For the last time, I'm fine, I can walk on my own,"" Alene growled at us when we got too protective of her ""I promise I won't let you see your child when he is born if you keep this up,"" she warned one more time and stride away from us.

She was happy to be our surrogate, she jumped at the chance to help us happy, when we were worried about the heir situation, it was brave of her to do this for us, her mate was open-minded and was honored to offer his mate's womb to us.

I looked at Alejandro who was still watching out for her, he was worried for the child because of his family curse but Cassandra assured us that the baby had no traces of the curse because he was my baby, Alejandro didn't care if the sperm was his or not he only cared about his health and that was all that mattered 

I Couldn't help but laugh when Alejandro walked to Alene and served her fruits for the hundredth time, I could hear her screaming her lungs out at him but it was funny to watch.

I smiled looking at my life, all the struggles, and wars we have been through we're finally out of our lives. this was happiness. this was home 

Alejandro was finally living the life he deserves and I was right next to him a place where I belong and now there was additional happiness in our little world. our son, he will be here any moment completing our little family.

I finally found my happily ever after

THE END"
